
# CloudBreach Incident Analysis ‚Äì AWS Account 238233324971

## üìÖ Incident Timeline (UTC)

| Time                      | Event Description                                                                 |
|---------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 2025-03-04T22:02:15       | Custom CloudWatch alarm triggered                                                  |
| 2025-03-04T22:05:27       | Billing alarm triggered due to abnormal spending                                  |
| 2025-03-04T23:59:15       | CloudFormation `ListStacks` call from external IP 76.147.57.220                    |
| 2025-03-04T23:59:09‚Äì39    | S3 `PutObject` operations into CloudTrail log buckets (possible tampering/persist) |

---

## üîê Root Cause
- Compromised IAM Access Key was exposed via a publicly accessible S3 bucket.
- The key was used to assume an **Admin** role.

---

## üîç Observed Actions by Attacker

- `AssumeRole` into `Admin` ‚Äì privilege escalation.
- `ListStacks` in AWS CloudFormation ‚Äì indicates reconnaissance behavior.
- `PutObject` in S3 ‚Äì likely targeting CloudTrail buckets to obscure activity or inject malicious artifacts.

---

## üìç Indicators of Compromise

| Field         | Details                                             |
|---------------|-----------------------------------------------------|
| IP Address    | `76.147.57.220`                                     |
| IAM Role      | `arn:aws:sts::238233324971:assumed-role/Admin/...`  |
| Event Types   | `AssumeRole`, `ListStacks`, `PutObject`             |
| Services Used | IAM, S3, CloudFormation                             |

---

## ‚úÖ Actions Taken

- Deleted compromised IAM Access Key
- Investigated CloudTrail logs from `2025-03-04T22:00` to `2025-03-05T00:00`
- Generated alert via billing and custom CloudWatch triggers

---

## üõ° Recommendations

### Immediate
- Review CloudFormation stack history
- Inspect S3 buckets (esp. CloudTrail logs) for unauthorized changes

### Short Term
- Rotate all credentials used for dev/test integration
- Harden S3 bucket policies to **deny public access**

### Long Term
- Enforce least privilege policies and IAM role boundaries
- Implement session tagging and automated detection for anomalous activity
- Use AWS Config for continuous compliance and visibility

---
